parallel architectures: a legacy implementation with separate SotW and Delta implementations, and a unified template-based implementation.\\n\\n## Core Components:\\n\\n### 1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl Adapter (grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc)\\nThe main adapter class that implements the `Config::Subscription` interface, serving as the bridge between xDS subscriptions (LDS, CDS, EDS, etc.) and the underlying GrpcMux implementation. This allows different resource types to multiplex onto a single gRPC stream.\\n\\n### 2. Legacy SotW Implementation (grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)\\nThe original State-of-the-World GrpcMuxImpl manages xDS v3 transport for SotW-style subscriptions using `DiscoveryRequest`/`DiscoveryResponse` protos. It handles wire-level concerns via `GrpcStream` and aggregates multiple subscriptions onto a single gRPC connection.\\n\\n### 3. Legacy Delta Implementation (new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)\\nThe NewGrpcMuxImpl implements incremental/delta xDS using `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`/`DeltaDiscoveryResponse` protos. This is the newer implementation that sends only resource changes rather than full state, and includes WatchMap for managing per-resource-type subscriptions. Supporting files include `delta_subscription_state.h/cc` for subscription state management.\\n\\n### 4. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory (grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc)\\nThe factory that creates GrpcSubscriptionImpl instances. It implements `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory` for SotW and `DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory` for Delta, selecting between the two based on configuration. The factory also instantiates the appropriate GrpcMux backend (legacy GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl or unified XdsMux variants).\\n\\n### 5. Unified XdsMux Template Implementation (xds_mux/)\\nA modern template-based unified implementation that supports both SotW and Delta variants through template specialization:\\n- `grpc_mux_impl.h/cc`: Contains the template `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` parameterized by subscription state type (S), factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). Concrete specializations are `GrpcMuxSotw` and `GrpcMuxDelta`.\\n- `subscription_state.h`: Base template `SubscriptionStateFactory<T>` for creating subscription states\\n- `sotw_subscription_state.h/cc`: `SotwSubscriptionState` and `SotwSubscriptionStateFactory` for SotW subscriptions\\n- `delta_subscription_state.h/cc`: `DeltaSubscriptionState` and `DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory` for Delta subscriptions\\n\\n### 6. Supporting Infrastructure:\\n- `watch_map.h/cc`: Manages watchers (subscribers) for a single resource type, implementing SubscriptionCallbacks interface\\n- `grpc_stream.h`: Low-level gRPC streaming interface for sending/receiving xDS proto messages\\n- `grpc_stream_interface.h`: Abstract interface for gRPC streams\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h`: Context object passed to mux implementations containing dispatcher, async client, and other configuration\\n- `grpc_mux_failover.h`: Failover support for primary/secondary xDS management servers\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.h/cc`: Manages acknowledgment queuing with pause/resume support\\n- `update_ack.h`: Represents an acknowledgment to be sent back to the xDS server\\n- `xds_source_id.h/cc`: Identifies xDS resource sources for per-source tracking\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.h/cc`: EDS-specific resource caching implementation\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.h/cc`: Factory for xDS-TP collection-based subscriptions\\n\\n### 7. Base Interfaces:\\n- `envoy/config/grpc_mux.h`: The GrpcMux interface that both legacy and unified implementations implement, along with `GrpcStreamCallbacks<ResponseProto>` template for stream callbacks\\n- `source/common/config/null_grpc_mux_impl.h`: Null implementation of GrpcMux when no ADS is configured\\n- `envoy/config/xds_resources_delegate.h`: Extension interface for hooking into xDS resource fetch events\\n\\n## Architecture Notes:\\nEnvoy is transitioning from dual implementations (legacy `GrpcMuxImpl`/`NewGrpcMuxImpl`) toward the unified XdsMux template-based approach. The `grpc_subscription_factory.cc` selects between implementations via runtime feature flags (e.g., `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux`). Both approaches implement the same public `GrpcMux` interface, allowing seamless switching at runtime. The unified implementation uses template specialization to support both SotW and Delta without code duplication, with `GrpcMuxSotw` and `GrpcMuxDelta` as concrete subclasses.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":7012,"cache_read_input_tokens":73091,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":7012},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"94d88491-1d84-41e7-a950-f9b301a65869","uuid":"4344c52d-8dfe-45d6-8338-8966867fbcd1"}

parallel architectures: a legacy implementation with separate SotW and Delta implementations, and a unified template-based implementation.\\n\\n## Core Components:\\n\\n### 1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl Adapter (grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc)\\nThe main adapter class that implements the `Config::Subscription` interface, serving as the bridge between xDS subscriptions (LDS, CDS, EDS, etc.) and the underlying GrpcMux implementation. This allows different resource types to multiplex onto a single gRPC stream.\\n\\n### 2. Legacy SotW Implementation (grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)\\nThe original State-of-the-World GrpcMuxImpl manages xDS v3 transport for SotW-style subscriptions using `DiscoveryRequest`/`DiscoveryResponse` protos. It handles wire-level concerns via `GrpcStream` and aggregates multiple subscriptions onto a single gRPC connection.\\n\\n### 3. Legacy Delta Implementation (new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)\\nThe NewGrpcMuxImpl implements incremental/delta xDS using `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`/`DeltaDiscoveryResponse` protos. This is the newer implementation that sends only resource changes rather than full state, and includes WatchMap for managing per-resource-type subscriptions. Supporting files include `delta_subscription_state.h/cc` for subscription state management.\\n\\n### 4. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory (grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc)\\nThe factory that creates GrpcSubscriptionImpl instances. It implements `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory` for SotW and `DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory` for Delta, selecting between the two based on configuration. The factory also instantiates the appropriate GrpcMux backend (legacy GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl or unified XdsMux variants).\\n\\n### 5. Unified XdsMux Template Implementation (xds_mux/)\\nA modern template-based unified implementation that supports both SotW and Delta variants through template specialization:\\n- `grpc_mux_impl.h/cc`: Contains the template `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` parameterized by subscription state type (S), factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). Concrete specializations are `GrpcMuxSotw` and `GrpcMuxDelta`.\\n- `subscription_state.h`: Base template `SubscriptionStateFactory<T>` for creating subscription states\\n- `sotw_subscription_state.h/cc`: `SotwSubscriptionState` and `SotwSubscriptionStateFactory` for SotW subscriptions\\n- `delta_subscription_state.h/cc`: `DeltaSubscriptionState` and `DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory` for Delta subscriptions\\n\\n### 6. Supporting Infrastructure:\\n- `watch_map.h/cc`: Manages watchers (subscribers) for a single resource type, implementing SubscriptionCallbacks interface\\n- `grpc_stream.h`: Low-level gRPC streaming interface for sending/receiving xDS proto messages\\n- `grpc_stream_interface.h`: Abstract interface for gRPC streams\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h`: Context object passed to mux implementations containing dispatcher, async client, and other configuration\\n- `grpc_mux_failover.h`: Failover support for primary/secondary xDS management servers\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.h/cc`: Manages acknowledgment queuing with pause/resume support\\n- `update_ack.h`: Represents an acknowledgment to be sent back to the xDS server\\n- `xds_source_id.h/cc`: Identifies xDS resource sources for per-source tracking\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.h/cc`: EDS-specific resource caching implementation\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.h/cc`: Factory for xDS-TP collection-based subscriptions\\n\\n### 7. Base Interfaces:\\n- `envoy/config/grpc_mux.h`: The GrpcMux interface that both legacy and unified implementations implement, along with `GrpcStreamCallbacks<ResponseProto>` template for stream callbacks\\n- `source/common/config/null_grpc_mux_impl.h`: Null implementation of GrpcMux when no ADS is configured\\n- `envoy/config/xds_resources_delegate.h`: Extension interface for hooking into xDS resource fetch events\\n\\n## Architecture Notes:\\nEnvoy is transitioning from dual implementations (legacy `GrpcMuxImpl`/`NewGrpcMuxImpl`) toward the unified XdsMux template-based approach. The `grpc_subscription_factory.cc` selects between implementations via runtime feature flags (e.g., `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux`). Both approaches implement the same public `GrpcMux` interface, allowing seamless switching at runtime. The unified implementation uses template specialization to support both SotW and Delta without code duplication, with `GrpcMuxSotw` and `GrpcMuxDelta` as concrete subclasses.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
